 aapako bhi himmat aegi jab us daur main log adaalat kii seedhiyaan chadh gaye to aap kyon hichak rahe hai
 In doing so, they gave an opportunity for the courts to be elevated because if it were not so, the politics of the court would have revolved between lawyers and governments and the democracy of India would not have expanded through the court
 ham bade vakeelon ko jaanate hai magar saadhaaran vakeelon ne bhi isamen badi bhoomika nibhaai he
 There was no shortage of lawyers in India at the time the Constitution was implemented
 jab bharat azaad hua tab 72,425 vakil the
 In terms of population, the number may be less, but India had the largest number of lawyers after America in the world
 1957 main jab china azaad hua tab vahaan maatr 3000 vakil the
 It is not that this process has stopped today, people have become shy about their rights
 balki jo buniyaad us vaqt padi thi usee kaa nateeja he ki aaj bhi aise vakil hai jo aam logon ke adhikaron kii ladaai ke liye aage aa jate hai or apane samay main samvidhan or uski aatma ko dhadkate rahane ke liye oxigen kii kami nahin hone dete hai
 The comments kerala kii ek aam ladki haadia shaktishaalee enie ke kilaaf apana mukadmaa lekar supreme court aa jaati he
 She counteracts the bogus concept of love jihad, despite the violent language of the news channels, she climbs up the stairs of the Supreme Court, fights and wins the case
 sirf enie ke kilaaf hi nahin balki kerala hycourt ke faisale ke kilaaf bhi jisamen uski shaadi ko amaanya kar diya gaya tha

 Who were those people who challenged their own elected government in the first few months after the constitution came into force
 ve pehle hi maheene main yaad dilaa rahe the ki thik he, hamane is sarkaar ke liye dedh sau saal sangharsh kiya he, is sarkaar main vahi log hai jinke peeche ham chalaa karte the, jail jaaya karte the lekin samvidhan kii bhaavana samvidhan kii bhaavana hoti he
 Will not compromise with this hazaron kii sankhya main log apane adhikaron ke hanan ke sawaal ko lekar adaalat pahunch gaye the, yah sankhya dekhakar lagata nahin ki bharat kii janata ne apane jivan main kabhi samvidhan dekha hi nahin tha
 They too had increased the lawsuit against the state

 fedral court of india 1937 main bana tha jo sirf teen jajon se chalata tha

 inhen 12 saalon main america kii sarvocch adaalat main maatr 960 cese hi sune gaye the

 In 1950, more than 600 writ petitions were heard in the Supreme Court
 jabaki uske pehle british fedral court ne 11 saal main maatr 169 keson ko hi suna tha
 The Federal Court of India was formed in 1937, which was run by only three judges
 1962 tak supreme court main suni jane vaali yachikaaon kii sankhya 3,833 ho gai thi
 In these 12 years, only 960 cases were heard in the Supreme Court of America
 america kii sarvocch adaalat kaa itihaas 100 saal se zyaada ho chukaa tha
 The courts were giving instructions to the governments while deciding on the writ petition, due to which there was growing uneasiness within the governments that it is its own people, it is a case against us, not only that ordinary people of India from the state i
e
 government The case started winning
 kya yah sundar or dilachasp nahin he ki samvidhan lagu hone ke kuch hi hafton or maheenon main ise logon ne apana liya or iske liye jeene-marane lage
 Within 15 years of the enactment of the Constitution, two-thirds of the lawsuits had citizens and the government face to face
 40 pratishat se adhik keson main log sarkaar se mukadmaa jeet gaye

 duniya main aisi kam hi sarkarein hongi jo janata ke saamne apane banaae kaanoonon kaa bachaav nahin kar sakin
